> ¹ Path, road

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*innü|*innü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nü|*nü]]_ ("see").
> ¹ Eye
### innya
[ɪnnjɑ]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*innya|*innya]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nya|*nya]]_ ("sound").
> ¹ Ear
### inpū
[ɪnpuː]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*inpū|*inpū]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pū|*pū]]_ ("elder sibling").
> ¹ Elder sibling; ² The larger of the two moons of Winter
### inqrus

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*inqrus|*inqrus]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*in-|*in-]]_ ("characteristic agent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qrus|*qrus]]_ ("day").
> ¹ The sun

### kyanīt
[kjɑniːt]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyanīt|*kyanīt]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kya-|*kya-]]_ ("suddenly or accidentally") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nīt|*nīt]]_ ("idea, thought").
> ¹ Idea
### kyaq'ay
[kjɑqʼɑj]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyaq'ay|*kyaq'ay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kya-|*kya-]]_ ("suddenly or accidentally") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'ay|*q'ay]]_ ("fall").
> ¹ To fall off; ² To fall over; ³ To collapse
### kyat'ay
[kjɑtʼɑj]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyat'ay|*kyat'ay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kya-|*kya-]]_ ("suddenly or accidentally") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ay|*t'ay]]_ ("be gone").
> ¹ To disappear
### kyawih
[kjɑwɪx]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyawih|*kyawih]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kya-|*kya-]]_ ("suddenly or accidentally") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wih|*wih]]_ ("alive").
> ¹ To come to life
### kyawik'
[kjɑwɪkʼ]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyawik'|*kyawik']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kya-|*kya-]]_ ("suddenly or accidentally") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wik'|*wik']]_ ("different, change").
> ¹ To change (suddenly or unexpectedly)
### kyawkyaw
[kjɑwkjɑw]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyawkyaw|*kyawkyaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyaw|*kyaw]]_ ("scream") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("repetitively").
> ¹ To caw, howl
### kyücyüc'
[kjʏtɕjʏtɕʼ]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyücyüc'|*kyücyüc']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyüc'|*kyüc']]_ ("rise") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("repetitively").
> ¹ To climb

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*patku|*patku]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pat'|*pat']]_ ("colour") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ku|*-ku]]_ ("-ness").
> ¹ Colour, hue
### paǖ
[pɑyː]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*paǖ|*paǖ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ|*ǖ]]_ ("wood, wooden").
> ¹ Tree
### pawü
[pɑwʏ]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pawü|*pawü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wüʔ|*wüʔ]]_ ("omen, luck").
> ¹ Omen
### payal
[pɑjɑl]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*payal|*payal]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pal|*pal]]_ ("wax, flow, accumulate").
> ¹ The first half of a _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#omö|omö]]_
### payya
[pɑjjɑ]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*payyaʔ|*payyaʔ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pyaʔ|*pyaʔ]]_ ("random, erratic").
> ¹ Random or unexpected event; ² Anomaly

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*surīg|*surīg]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sur|*sur]]_ ("submerge") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*īg|*īg]]_ ("enter").
> ¹ To dive into water
### surüp
[sʊʁʏp]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*surüp|*surüp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ur>|*<ur>]]_ ("quick and repetitive for a short time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*süp|*süp]]_ ("carve").
> ¹ To carve (wood)
### surūm
[sʊʁuːm]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*surūm|*surūm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ur>|*<ur>]]_ ("quick and repetitive for a short time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sūm|*sūm]]_ ("remove").
> ¹ To sift
### suta
[sʊtɑ]
*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*suta|*suta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sut|*sut]]_ ("blue, green").
> ¹ Blue, green
### sutcayic
[sʊttɕɑjɪtɕ]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sutcayic|*sutcayic]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sut|*sut]]_ ("blue, green") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cay|*cay]]_ ("pass by") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ic|*-ic]]_ ("agentive").
> ¹ A green comet which appears in Winter's sky every few centuries
### sǖca
[syːtɕɑ]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'eqya|*t'eqya]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'eq|*t'eq]]_ ("egg") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-i|*-i]]_ ("physically similar").
> ¹ Spherical, egg-shaped
### t'iwra
[tʼɪwʁɑ]
*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'iwga|*t'iwga]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'i|*t'i]]_ ("small") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ug|*-ug]]_ ("augmentative").
> ¹ Tiny
### t'īqim
[tʼiːqɪm]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'īqem|*t'īqem]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'eq|*t'eq]]_ ("egg") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Nest of a bird
### t'urik
[tʼʊʁɪk]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'urik|*t'urik]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ur>|*<ur>]]_ ("quick and repetitive for a short time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ik|*t'ik]]_ ("cut").
> ¹ To cut up into pieces, as of fabric or leafy vegetables
### t'ükt'ük'
[tʼʏktʼʏkʼ]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ükt'ük'|*t'ükt'ük']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ük'|*t'ük']]_ ("chop up") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("repetitively").
> ¹ To chop up into pieces, as of meat
### t'ūc'ah
[tʼuːtɕʼɑχ]

### t'ūgǖ
[tʼuːɣyː]

> ¹ The [[T'ugü]] river basin, the entire world known to the [[Öb]] before contact with other cultures

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖcīk'|*ǖcīk']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cīk'|*cīk']]_ ("tip").
> ¹ To be at the tip of
### ǖgǖm
[yːɣyːm]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖhǖm|*ǖhǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hǖm|*hǖm]]_ ("upstream of, before").
> ¹ To be uphill, upstream of; ² To be before
### ǖgwac
[yːɣwɑtɕ]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖgwac|*ǖgwac]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gwac|*gwac]]_ ("far away").
> ¹ To be far away from
### ǖkīs
[yːkiːs]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖkīs|*ǖkīs]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ-|*ǖ-]]_ ("locative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kīs|*kīs]]_ ("top, on top").
> ¹ To be on top of
### ǖm
[yːm]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖm|*ǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖ|*ǖ]]_ ("wood, wooden") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ A complex construction made from several pieces of wood
> **Derivatives:** _[[High Alöbi dictionary#q'aq'ugǖmi|q'aq'ugǖmi]]_ ("wagon house")
### ǖmwit'

### wīxa
[wiːɕɑ]
*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wīxa|*wīxa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wīx|*wīx]]_ ("sacred, shining"). Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*plīxma|*plīxma]]_ ("shining").
> ¹ Sacred; ² Relating to light in spiritual or theological contexts
### wuk'i
[wʊkʼɪ]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wuk'i|*wuk'i]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wu-|*wu-]]_ ("back and forth") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'i|*k'i]]_ ("hang, swing").
> ¹ To swing
### wupay
[wʊpɑj]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wupay|*wupay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wu-|*wu-]]_ ("back and forth") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pay|*pay]]_ ("layer").
> ¹ To coat in paint
### wuqam
[wʊqɑm]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wukam|*wukam]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wu-|*wu-]]_ ("back and forth") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kam|*kam]]_ ("wash").
> ¹ To wash, as of clothes
### wuraw
[wʊʁɑw]

> ¹ To weave
### wurǖt
[wʊʁyːt]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wurǖt|*wurǖt]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wuraw|*wuraw]]_ ("to weave") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Basket

### yiqicug
[jɪqɪtɕʊɣ]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yeqicug|*yeqicug]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yeqic|*yeqic]]_ ("rodent") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ug|*-ug]]_ ("augmentative").
> ¹ [[Iqicog]], a large rodent endemic to [[T'ugü]], similar to the capybara
### yira
[jɪʁɑ]
*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yiha|*yiha]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yih|*yih]]_ ("feather").
> ¹ Feathered; ² Ornately decorated
### yīwan
[jiːwɑn]
*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yīwan|*yīwan]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<īw>|*<īw>]]_ ("internal organ") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yan|*yan]]_ ("within, inside").
> ¹ Stomach
### yugül
[jʊɣʏl]
*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yuhül|*yuhül]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yu-|*yu-]]_ ("passively") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hül|*hül]]_ ("sleep").
> ¹ To sleep
